## Why It Matters
Source signal: <h3>Highlights</h3>
<ul>
<li><strong>More reliable agent turns and session state:</strong> OpenClaw now preserves pending subagent completion announcements, keeps chat history transcripts non-empty, maintains media index alignment, restarts dormant follow-up drains, and resolves compaction model aliases consistently. <h3>Fixes</h3>
